# Italian Text Review — splnit.eu
Language: Italian
Source file: messages/it-IT.json + hardcoded sources
Prepared for: specialist review
Instructions for reviewer: Use the KEY or SOURCE reference exactly as written when returning corrections.

---

## How to use this document

For each string below:
- If the text is correct, write: OK
- If the text needs a change, write the corrected version directly below the current text, prefixed with: CORRECTION:
- If context is needed before deciding, write: QUERY: [your question]

Return the completed document. Do not change the KEY or SOURCE lines — these are used to apply your corrections back to the app.

---
